                FOOD TIMELINE QUESTIONS  March 1999-January 31, 2015

This is the complete catalog of questions answered by the FT reference & research service.
Most of our work is not (yet) uploaded to the Internet. Online answers(FAQ) may be accessed here: 
http://www.foodtimeline.org/foodfaqindex.html 
How to read this catalog: question, [number of times asked] date answered. Our answers stored in paper files and/or electronic
format. If you need anything from this catalog let us know. If you don't see the answer to your question, send it in. We love
new challenges. Service is FREE and welcomes everyone! 

Lynne Olver, editor
The Food Timeline 
foodtimeline@aol.com
************************
